#   `embedder.py` sample progress        #
#   (general idea for category filter)   #
#                                        #
##########################################
"""
Embedding manager for category-based product filtering.

Uses sentence-transformers to classify user messages into product categories,
enabling efficient pre-filtering before LLM-based recommendation.
"""

import numpy as np
import pickle
from pathlib import Path
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity


# Category descriptions optimized for semantic matching
CATEGORY_DESCRIPTIONS = {
    "Running Shoes": "running shoes jogging marathon training sneakers footwear athletic",
    "Yoga": "yoga mat blocks meditation stretching flexibility exercise poses",
    "Laptops": "laptop computer macbook notebook portable pc work college",
    "Electronics": "charger cable adapter power usb electronics accessories",
    "Headphones": "headphones earbuds audio music listening noise cancelling wireless",
    "Outerwear": "jacket coat fleece rain winter warm outdoor clothing layers",
    "Water Bottles": "water bottle tumbler hydration flask insulated drinks",
    "Kitchen": "kitchen cooking appliances mixer air fryer instant pot food processor",
    "Fitness": "fitness workout gym exercise weights dumbbells resistance muscle recovery",
    "Camping": "camping tent sleeping bag outdoor hiking backpacking gear",
    "Wearables": "smartwatch fitness tracker watch wearable health tracking",
    "Audio": "microphone audio recording podcast studio sound",
    "Workwear": "work boots gloves pants jacket construction durable",
    "Tablets": "tablet ipad android reading notes drawing portable screen",
    "Home": "home vacuum cleaner thermostat doorbell smart home cleaning",
}

CACHE_PATH = Path(__file__).parent / ".cache" / "category_embeddings.pkl"


class CategoryEmbedder:
    """Embeds product categories for message classification."""

    def __init__(self, model_name: str = "all-MiniLM-L6-v2"):
        self.model = SentenceTransformer(model_name)
        self.category_embeddings: dict[str, np.ndarray] = {}

    def build_cache(self) -> None:
        """Compute category embeddings and save to cache."""
        print("Computing category embeddings...")
        for category, description in CATEGORY_DESCRIPTIONS.items():
            self.category_embeddings[category] = self.model.encode(description)

        CACHE_PATH.parent.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        with open(CACHE_PATH, "wb") as f:
            pickle.dump(self.category_embeddings, f)
        print(f"Cached {len(self.category_embeddings)} categories to {CACHE_PATH}")

    def load_cache(self) -> None:
        """Load category embeddings from cache. Raises if cache doesn't exist."""
        if not CACHE_PATH.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(
                f"Cache not found at {CACHE_PATH}. Run 'python embed.py' first."
            )

        with open(CACHE_PATH, "rb") as f:
            self.category_embeddings = pickle.load(f)

    def get_top_categories(self, message: str, top_k: int = 2) -> list[tuple[str, float]]:
        """
        Get the top-k most relevant categories for a user message.

        Returns list of (category_name, similarity_score) tuples.
        """
        if not self.category_embeddings:
            raise RuntimeError("No embeddings loaded. Call load_cache() first.")

        message_embedding = self.model.encode(message)

        similarities = {}
        for category, cat_embedding in self.category_embeddings.items():
            sim = cosine_similarity([message_embedding], [cat_embedding])[0][0]
            similarities[category] = float(sim)

        sorted_categories = sorted(similarities.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return sorted_categories[:top_k]

    @staticmethod
    def clear_cache() -> None:
        """Remove cached embeddings."""
        if CACHE_PATH.exists():
            CACHE_PATH.unlink()
            print("Cache cleared.")
        else:
            print("No cache to clear.")
